Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: daisy\\ \tt RIGHT: rose\\ \tt TOP: banana\\ \tt BOTTOM: elephant\\ \tt CENTER: aluminium\\ \tt NORTHWEST: accordion\\ \tt NORTHEAST: horse\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: butterfly\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: mimosa\\ \tt HERE: saxophone\\ \tt THERE: iron\\ \tt NOWHERE: ukulele\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: eagle\\ \tt INSIDE: pansy\\ \tt OUTSIDE: lizard\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start.
